# QA Matrix

> 文件狀態：Active quality doc
>
> 本文件是 Infinite Pro 唯一的 living QA matrix。所有 shipped verification evidence 都應追加在這裡，而不是再建立新的 QA matrix 檔案。

This file is the single living QA matrix for Infinite Pro.

Maintenance rule:
- keep all new QA evidence in this file
- add dated sections inside this file instead of creating a new QA matrix file by default
- only update when build / typecheck / smoke / test evidence actually exists

---

## Entry: 2026-03-30 baseline workbench pass

Verification posture:
- real backend + real frontend
- browser-driven interaction on local runtime
- non-destructive actions prioritized first
- destructive / cleanup actions intentionally excluded unless explicitly requested

Environment used:
- frontend: `http://127.0.0.1:3001`
- backend: `http://127.0.0.1:8010/api/v1`
- database: local `acceptance.db`

Important runtime note:
- When building frontend for local QA, keep `NEXT_PUBLIC_API_BASE_URL=http://127.0.0.1:8010/api/v1`
- If omitted, the client bundle can fall back to `:8000`, which may point at a different backend/runtime

### Verified

| Area | Page / Flow | Action | Status | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Intake | `/new` | Fill core question and create matter without materials | Verified | Redirects into matter workspace |
| Intake | `/new` | Create matter with URL + pasted text | Verified | Matter is created and materials are attached |
| Intake | `/new` | Non-ASCII URL request path handling | Verified | Unicode URL request normalization fixed in backend |
| Matter | `/matters/[matterId]` | Primary CTA `執行分析並打開交付物` | Verified | Creates deliverable and opens deliverable workspace |
| Matter | `/matters/[matterId]` | Write checkpoint | Verified | `Checkpoint 已寫回這個案件世界` |
| Matter | `/matters/[matterId]` | Keyboard tab navigation with ArrowRight | Verified | Tab selection moves correctly |
| Evidence | `/matters/[matterId]/evidence` | Add pasted follow-up material | Verified | Source/artifact/evidence counts update |
| Task | `/tasks/[taskId]` | Open focus task from evidence / history / matter | Verified | Page loads and linked deliverable path is usable |
| Deliverable | `/deliverables` | Open deliverable workspace from list | Verified | Opens correct deliverable workspace |
| Deliverable | `/deliverables/[deliverableId]` | Read latest deliverable after run | Verified | Correct deliverable content and provenance surface visible |
| History | `/history` | Open task / matter from history list | Verified | Navigation works |
| Matters list | `/matters` | Search by `MVP` | Verified | List narrows to the expected matter |
| Settings | `/settings` | Save workbench preferences | Verified | Success status shown and persisted remotely |
| Settings | `/settings` | Switch theme to dark | Verified | Remote + local state + shell theme now sync correctly |
| Settings | `/settings` | Enter provider edit mode | Verified | Edit mode and validation/apply controls appear |
| Agents | `/agents` | Open edit mode for Host agent | Verified | Host edit form opens |
| Agents | `/agents` | Save Host agent | Verified | `代理「Host Agent」已寫入正式管理狀態` |
| Packs | `/packs` | Switch to industry-pack tab | Verified | Tab / tabpanel switching works |
| Packs | `/packs` | Edit and save `Ecommerce Pack` | Verified | `模組包「Ecommerce Pack」已寫入正式管理狀態` |
| Shell | global | Skip link present | Verified | `跳到主要內容` is rendered |
| Shell | global | Main navigation across core pages | Verified | `/`, `/new`, `/matters`, `/deliverables`, `/agents`, `/packs`, `/history`, `/settings` |

### Verified Engineering Checks

| Check | Result |
| --- | --- |
| `python3 -m compileall backend/app` | Passed |
| `.venv312/bin/python -m pytest backend/tests` | Passed (`84 passed`) |
| `cd frontend && npm run build` | Passed |
| `cd frontend && npm run typecheck` | Passed after `.next/types` regenerated by build |

### Fixed During QA

| Issue | Result |
| --- | --- |
| Remote ingestion failed on Unicode URL paths / queries | Fixed in backend request normalization |
| Theme save did not propagate across same-tab workbench consumers | Fixed with in-tab persistent state sync event |

### Intentionally Not Tested In This Pass

These actions were left untouched because they change state in a destructive or cleanup-heavy way:

- history page `清理本頁`
- history page `清空全部歷史入口`
- agent `停用`
- pack `停用`
- provider `強制儲存`
- provider runtime validation against altered credentials

### Residual Notes

- A specific third-party Chinese URL can now be requested safely, but may still return a legitimate ingest failure if the site itself is not parse-friendly or readable in practice.
- Local QA is sensitive to which backend port the frontend bundle is built against.

| `cd frontend && npm run build` | Passed |

### Wave 3 specific verification

| Area | Page / Flow | Action | Status | Notes |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Backend | upload / source ingest | Text-first material creates `ChunkObject` rows | Verified | `source_chunk` evidence now points to `chunk_object_id` |
| Backend | upload / source ingest | Limited-support image creates `MediaReference` | Verified | Evidence stays reference-level and points to `media_reference_id` |
| Backend | deliverable support chain | Deliverable linked evidence includes chunk-backed provenance | Verified | At least one deliverable chain resolves to `chunk_object` |
| Evidence | `/matters/[matterId]/evidence` | Expand `證據支撐鏈` and inspect provenance disclosure | Verified | Shows `引用來源片段`, chunk locator, excerpt, and `引用媒體參照` for limited-support material |
| Task | `/tasks/[taskId]` | Expand `證據與補充資料` and inspect provenance disclosure | Verified | Chunk/media provenance visible only in disclosure |
| Deliverable | `/deliverables/[deliverableId]` | Expand support-chain detail and inspect linked evidence provenance | Verified | Deliverable can trace back to chunk-backed evidence without polluting hero |

- evidence can now expose a more precise support point below source-level

- limited-support / unsupported materials remain honest and reference-level
- first-screen primary flows stayed intact on evidence / task / deliverable surfaces

| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

| Packs UI | `/packs` | Disclosure shows interface ids, required-property gaps, and rule bindings | Verified | details stay behind disclosure, not on first-screen hero |

| Matter UI | `/matters/[matterId]` | First-screen matter hero remains consultant-first | Verified | no contract metadata pollution on the main task/matter first screen |

- failing case replay source: `/tmp/p0c_batch2_run.json`
- aggregate snapshot used for replay: `/tmp/p0d0_task_aggregate.json`

  - `/tmp/operations_payload.json`
  - `/tmp/strategy_business_analysis_payload.json`

### Verified outcomes

- the `finance_capital` runtime issue was narrowed to a provider-side parse-body `HTTP 400` failure mode rather than a pack-layer or deliverable-writeback bug
- the official OpenAI path now does a local request-body preflight before the network call
- if the local request body is valid but OpenAI returns the specific parse-body `HTTP 400`, the provider retries once on the same governed path instead of failing immediately
- the fix stays fail-closed after the retry and does not bypass Host orchestration or the provider abstraction boundary

- the active UX spec now explicitly requires consultant-friendly, low-jargon copy
- some deeper technical or data-derived strings still remain in lower-level disclosures and form diagnostics; they should be handled in a later copy pass if full zero-English visible polish is required

- remaining English visible in the product may still come from:

  - seeded test/demo data

- `matter / evidence` 會直接把旗艦流程的姿態、邊界與升級條件講清楚
- `task / deliverable` 也能沿用同一套旗艦閱讀，但維持在較低噪音的工作面深層，不讓首屏變成資訊牆
- document-heavy review workflow 現在不只在 hero 口徑上對齊，也能在交付物深層閱讀中穩定說清楚「目前是 review memo / assessment，而不是最終決策版本」

### Runtime observations from the authenticated pass

- The first authenticated run (`supplemental` external-search posture) logged an external-search timeout before continuing and eventually persisted the result.
- The second authenticated run (`不用，我只想用我提供的資料`) skipped the external-search branch, produced structured outputs, and reached the deliverable workspace in the browser.
- No browser console errors were observed on the authenticated overview, matter, or deliverable surfaces during the validated paths.

### Important honesty note

- this pass intentionally downgrades the earlier evidence-upload claim from `Verified` to `Limited`
- the reason is not that the visible trigger disappeared; it is that protected-route browser automation only confirmed chooser opening, not a stable end-to-end pending-material list update
- implementation parity and regression tests still confirm that `/new` and `/matters/[matterId]/evidence` share the same explicit upload-trigger structure
- as in earlier passes, the stable verification order for this repo remains `build -> typecheck`; running them in parallel can still transiently fail on regenerated `.next/types`
